2026-06-12 · Session 53 (live market-open observability verification uncovered a TOTAL capture + compute blackout — root-caused to a cron SHELL-directive loss and recovered to a clean self-running pipeline in one live session) · PASS · **Trigger:** S52's market-open test at 09:30 IST found script_execution_log showing 0 shadow_runner rows, status.json frozen at 01:32 UTC, capture tables 0 rows. After several falsified hypotheses (missing logs/ dir; reboot; cron daemon down; .env corruption; permissions — each killed by the next probe), a cron probe proved cron was running jobs under `SHELL=/bin/sh` (dash). **ROOT CAUSE:** a crontab reinstall at 00:47 UTC 2026-06-12 dropped the `SHELL=/bin/bash` directive → cron defaulted to /bin/sh (dash) → `source` is a bash builtin dash lacks → every `cd … && source .env && python3 …` chain died with `/bin/sh: source: not found` into discarded cron mail ("No MTA installed"), silently, since ~2026-06-11 05:03 UTC. Capture AND all four S52 monitors share that exact `source .env` chain → all died identically (watchdog and patient dying together). **SECONDARY casualty of the same 00:47 reinstall:** the four run_ingest.sh crontab lines were corrupted (command body lost) so option-chain ingest never ran. **FIXES DEPLOYED LIVE (all verified):** (1) added `SHELL=/bin/bash` as crontab line 1 via `crontab -e` — resurrected capture + all 4 monitors within ~80s; (2) reconstructed the 4 ingest lines to the working UNQUOTED form `cd … && bash run_ingest.sh NIFTY/SENSEX FULL >> cron.log 2>&1` (run_ingest.sh self-sources .env; the S49 single-quoted 'NIFTY FULL' form is NOT what's live — the unquoted form is, confirmed by 248+ INGEST OPTION CHAIN COMPLETED); (3) commented out the two capture_index_futures_snapshot_local.py cron lines — hard SyntaxError at lines 246/253 (`path.relative_to(Path(r'C:\GammaEnginePython'))` — backslash inside f-string expr + Windows path; never ran on AWS) → futures DARK pending fix; (4) volatility 409 fix: compute_volatility_metrics_local.py changed `sb.insert(TARGET_TABLE, [row])` → `sb.upsert(TARGET_TABLE, [row], on_conflict="symbol,ts")` (core/supabase_client.py already had upsert with Prefer: resolution=merge-duplicates; the insert-not-upsert was punted "out of scope for ENH-72", not deliberate). Deployed via Local Notepad edit → commit cd98a87 → EC2 `git checkout origin/main -- compute_volatility_metrics_local.py` (full pull blocked by a mass-CRLF-flip dirty tree; targeted checkout used, NOT full pull). Verified live: sb.upsert on disk, COMPILE OK, PIPELINE COMPLETE, no 23505. **TDs filed S53: 6** — TD-S53-NEW-1 SHELL/dash root cause (RESOLVED); TD-S53-NEW-2 ingest-line corruption (RESOLVED); TD-S53-NEW-3 compute_volatility_metrics lacked ON CONFLICT → 409 collisions (RESOLVED via upsert); TD-S53-NEW-4 ingest :00–29 schedule hole (carried to S54, CLOSED there via */5); TD-S53-NEW-5 S2 S52 monitors report false state (999 age-clamp reads STALE on fresh tables; false-negative "no orchestrator in last 5 min" after a confirmed run; watchdog shares the same source-.env failure chain as the systems it watches) — OPEN; TD-S53-NEW-6 S2 futures script Windows-path SyntaxError line 246/253 — OPEN. **TDs closed S53: 3 same-session** (NEW-1/2/3). **0 ADRs** (Rule 10 excludes bug-fixes from mandatory ADRs). **0 ENH.** **Git:** commit cd98a87 (volatility upsert); EC2 working tree filthy with ~200 CRLF-flipped false-Modified files → targeted `git checkout origin/main -- <file>` is canonical here, never full pull. **CRITICAL LESSONS S53:** (a) **Always verify `SHELL=/bin/bash` as crontab line 1 on AWS** — cron defaulting to /bin/sh (dash) silently kills any job using `source`; the reliable probe is `/bin/sh -c 'source .env && echo CHAIN_OK'` + `pwd; echo HOME=$HOME; SHELL=$SHELL`. (b) **Never deploy monitors that share the failure chain of what they monitor** — all four S52 monitors used the same `source .env` prefix and died with the capture layer (watchdog + patient die together); monitor env-loading must be independent. (c) **The live ingest form is unquoted `bash run_ingest.sh NIFTY FULL`** — the script self-sources .env; do not reintroduce S49's single-quoted arg. (d) **Cron does not inherit shell env vars** — every job needs explicit env loading, and that requires bash not sh. **CARRY_FORWARD_TO_S54:** P0 NEW-4 ingest :00–29 hole fill (*/5 on the 04–09 lines); P1 futures SyntaxError fix (NEW-6); P1b monitor false-state fixes (NEW-5); P2 first-full-day data-integrity audit once Monday trades. · **PRODUCTION_PATCHES=1** (compute_volatility_metrics_local.py insert→upsert; commit cd98a87) · **CRON_CHANGES=3** (SHELL line added; 4 ingest lines reconstructed; 2 futures lines commented) · **TDs_CLOSED=3** (NEW-1/2/3 same-session) · **TDs_NEW=6** (TD-S53-NEW-1..6) · **ADRs_NEW=0** · **ENH_NEW=0** · **BLACKOUT_DURATION≈~28h** (2026-06-11 05:03 UTC → 2026-06-12 fix) · **ROOT_CAUSE=SHELL_directive_dropped_cron_defaulted_dash_source_builtin_absent** · **HOURS_OPERATOR=~4** · docs_updated:yes

2026-05-29 · `(pending S40 close commit)` · Session 40 (TD-S37-01 CLOSED via patch_s40_enh83_view_tau_rewrite.py runtime τ lookup + Marketview v4 atomic-card redesign through 4 mockup iterations APPLIED via Lovable + AWS deploy pipeline established via fresh clone at /home/ssm-user/meridian-connect + update_parameter RPC valid_to DEFAULT now() bug DISCOVERED + FIXED same-session + schema-mismatch correction prompt for Lovable column-name corrections + v_max_pain_by_strike long-format pivot view created and verified + 9-canonical-file doc-close pack per Doc Protocol v4 Rule 3 + Rule 9 + Rule 11 full-file no-crunch): **S40 primary mandate** = TD-S37-01 closure (P1 carry-forward from S39, hardcoded τ_pin=τ_accel=0.30 in ENH-81 views formalize as `merdian_parameters` lookup) + Marketview v4 polish driven by operator dashboard screenshots showing single-Hero rollup architecture violates ADR-017 P1 three-filter rule (Hero card collapses 4 distinct metrics into one paragraph — implicit metric placement + redundant repetition of net dealer γ in 3 cards + systemic mixed-grain of category labels and instances). **TD-S37-01 patch shipped via `patch_s40_enh83_view_tau_rewrite.py` (BOM-safe, predominant-EOL preservation, AST-validate, `_PRE_S40.sql` backups for both view DDL files, idempotency guard, ASCII-clean post cp1252 fix):** two surgical replacements of `0.3::numeric AS tau_pin` and `0.3::numeric AS tau_accel` with `get_parameter_num('pin.tau.'||p.symbol)::numeric AS tau_used` and `get_parameter_num('accel.tau.'||p.symbol)::numeric AS tau_used` respectively in `sql/2026-05-25_enh81_v_gex_strike_pin_zone.sql` and `sql/2026-05-25_enh81_v_gex_strike_accel_zone.sql`; dry-run PASS → live → both view DDLs re-applied via Supabase SQL editor → smoke-fire SQL verified `tau_used = 0.30` rendered correctly in both views for NIFTY + SENSEX cross-symbol against live `merdian_parameters` rows (`pin.tau.NIFTY=0.30`, `pin.tau.SENSEX=0.30`, `accel.tau.NIFTY=0.30`, `accel.tau.SENSEX=0.30` all from ENH-110 Phase 1 bootstrap seed). **TD-S40-NEW-2 DISCOVERED + FIXED same-session — `update_parameter()` SECURITY DEFINER RPC violated `chk_valid_from_to` CHECK constraint:** Root cause: Lovable's auto-scaffold gave `merdian_parameters.valid_to` column a `DEFAULT now()` value at table-create time; Postgres `now()` returns the transaction timestamp which is identical across all calls within a single transaction (statement_timestamp() differs only across transactions); when `update_parameter` ran atomic close-old-row (`SET valid_to=now()`) + insert-new-row (`valid_from default now(), valid_to default now()`) inside one transaction the new row got `valid_from = valid_to` → CHECK `chk_valid_from_to (valid_from < valid_to OR valid_to IS NULL)` rejected. Fix applied via Supabase SQL editor: `ALTER TABLE public.merdian_parameters ALTER COLUMN valid_to DROP DEFAULT;` — verified 0.30→0.25→0.30 round-trip on `pin.tau.NIFTY` with clean temporal chain (1st row valid_to=null, 2nd row 1st gets valid_to=t1 / new row valid_from=t1 valid_to=null, 3rd row 2nd gets valid_to=t2 / new row valid_from=t2 valid_to=null — strict chain). Codified as **D.22.1** (Lovable temporal-immutable column DEFAULT audit pattern — any column intended to differentiate by transaction-time within a single transaction must NOT carry `DEFAULT now()` or any statement-timestamp-equivalent default; subsequent Lovable schema scaffolds for temporal-immutable tables require pre-deploy `information_schema.columns` audit for `column_default IS NOT NULL AND column_default LIKE '%now()%'` on any column whose semantics span multiple rows within one transaction). **Marketview v4 atomic-card redesign — 4 mockup iterations through HTML→wkhtmltoimage render→operator feedback loop:** v1 (HTML 1,250 lines) replaced single-Hero rollup with 5-tile Key Parameters strip (Regime + Net Dealer γ + Spot Context + Flip Level + Max γ Strike) + separate Positioning Landscape + Max Pain side-by-side + Pin Risk Score/Probability/ATM Straddle row + Breadth & Volatility row + ICT Zones + Signals — operator feedback: \"Positioning and Max Pain side-by-side makes cross-reading impossible — strikes on x-axis don't align between charts\"; v2 stacked Positioning + Max Pain full-width with shared strike-axis range — operator feedback: \"PIN ZONE and ACCEL ZONE should be in the Key Parameters strip not buried in Positioning\"; v3 promoted PIN ZONE and ACCEL ZONE to Key Parameters (now 7 tiles compact); v4 final added Pin Risk Timeline as standalone row, demoted ICT Zones below Signals stream because zones are reference info not decision-driving (decision-tier metrics get top placement per ADR-017 P1) — final rendered to `/mnt/user-data/outputs/marketview_v4_mockup.html` + `marketview_v4_render.png` (wkhtmltoimage). Codified as **D.22.2** (atomic single-metric card layout VALIDATED — each card answers exactly ONE question; collapses-into-paragraph Hero cards violate the three-filter rule because the paragraph form prevents per-metric isolation under operator-scan). Codified as **D.22.3** (stacked-by-strike charts VALIDATED for cross-reading Positioning + Max Pain — vertical strike-axis alignment is mandatory when two charts measure different metrics over the same strike domain because horizontal side-by-side breaks the eye's ability to cross-reference 24,050 max-γ against 23,900 max-pain magnets — the 100pt convergent pin pressure signal is invisible side-by-side and obvious stacked). **Lovable build prompt authored at `/mnt/user-data/outputs/lovable_build_prompt_marketview_v4.md` (515 lines, ~3940 words):** structured with CONTEXT + hard constraints (\"render exactly the layout described below — do not invent extra cards or reorder sections\") + Step 0 (delete the Hero component first then rebuild) + design tokens (font scale 11/13/16/20/28 + neutral palette + zone color tokens green/red/yellow/blue) + 9 layout sections each with per-card Supabase wiring (table, columns, filter expression, refresh cadence) + v_max_pain_by_strike view DDL block as Appendix A + acceptance criteria (\"each card must show ONE metric headline + ONE sub-line context max\") + 7-phase incremental pasting option for operators who don't want to ship the whole prompt at once. P3b ADR-006 AWS migration scope draft (BLOCKED on TD-080 Dhan token refresh — un-actioned). P4 12 carry-forward TDs from S39 un-actioned. P5 older items (TD-NEW-B pg_cron health-check, TD-NEW-C/D/9 ws_feed bundle, TD-NEW-H NULL expiry, TD-073/074/087/094/095/099, ENH-95, S21+ uncommitted patches reconcile, S23 docs review pass). **CRITICAL LESSONS S40:** (a) **Lovable auto-scaffold DEFAULT values must be audited at table-create time for temporal-immutable semantics** — `now()` as a column default looks innocuous but breaks any RPC that needs different row-timestamps within a single transaction; `update_parameter`'s atomic close-old-insert-new pattern is the canonical temporal-immutable workflow and it required `valid_to DROP DEFAULT` to function; generalizable as: any column whose semantics differentiate rows by transaction-time within one transaction must NOT carry a transaction-timestamp default. (b) **Atomic single-metric cards beat collapsed Hero rollups for operator-scan decision surfaces** — D.22.2 codification of ADR-017 P1 three-filter rule operational form: each card answers ONE question; multi-metric paragraph-Hero cards fail because they prevent per-metric isolation during the 3-second scan that ADR-017 was designed to enable; when in doubt, split. (c) **Stacked-by-strike axis alignment is mandatory for cross-reading two charts over the same domain** — D.22.3 was discovered empirically when operator couldn't visually align max-γ 24,050 against max-pain 23,900 in v1 side-by-side layout; vertical stack with shared x-axis made the 100pt convergent pin pressure signal obvious; generalizable to any pair of charts measuring different metrics over a shared horizontal axis. (d) **Schema verification before Lovable column-name assumption is canonical workflow** — Lovable's column-name guesses were directionally reasonable but didn't match actual `gamma_metrics` schema; live curl with NIFTY filter to inspect ACTUAL columns is the cheap step that should precede any wiring prompt; codified as: any Lovable wiring prompt for a Supabase-backed dashboard must include the live column inventory as Appendix to prevent guess-and-iterate cycles. (e) **AWS clone + on-AWS build pipeline beats scp-of-built-html for ergonomic deploys** — pre-S40 deploy was operator scp'ing `dist/` from Lovable preview to AWS `/var/www/marketview/`; S40 codified the 3-line `git pull && npm run build && sudo rsync && sudo systemctl reload nginx` pipeline which costs ~45s wall-clock and is one command; the architectural shift is that source-of-truth lives in GitHub and AWS builds from source rather than receiving pre-built artifacts — generalizes to any frontend AWS deploy. (f) **Same-session DISCOVERED + FIXED TD-S40-NEW-2 demonstrates schema-defect detection via RPC smoke-fire** — the `chk_valid_from_to` violation only surfaced when calibration console attempted a parameter update; if S40 hadn't included a calibration round-trip smoke-fire, the bug would have persisted silent and broken the first operator-driven calibration attempt in S41+; canonical pattern is: any schema-add-constraints + RPC pair must include a same-session round-trip smoke-fire to surface CHECK-violation interactions. (g) **Writer-side empty-card detection on Marketview is a feature not a bug** — 4 cards correctly degraded to empty states (VIX, WCB, Pin Risk Score, Pin Risk Timeline) when their backing columns/tables were absent or NULL; the dashboard does not silently fabricate values; operator can immediately distinguish frontend wiring issues from writer-side gaps by which cards are empty; preserves the audit-trail discipline ADR-017 P3 asymmetric surfacing established. · **PRODUCTION_PATCHES=0** (S40 was SQL DDL + Lovable iterations + AWS deploy infra; RLS filters rows but GRANT lets the role attempt the operation; verification via 91-row anon-grants audit caught it before any exploitation; remediation pattern is `REVOKE ALL + GRANT SELECT` in PL/pgSQL loop across all surfaces; future Lovable schema/grant operations require pre-deploy anon-grants audit. (b) **Schema-iteration drift between checks is real and silent** — within S39 the operator pasted `information_schema.columns` for merdian_parameters TWICE; first paste showed single `value jsonb` column, second paste (after Lovable rebuild) showed 4 typed columns; SQL written against first-paste schema failed `42703: column "value" does not exist` even though `value` clearly appeared in the column list — Lovable had silently rebuilt the table between schema check and SQL apply; pattern is `verify schema immediately before each ALTER/SELECT against Lovable-managed tables` not once-per-session. (c) **AWS Security Group attached to EC2 != SG operator is editing** — operator edited launch-wizard-2 inbound rules for hours; canonical fix via IMDSv2 token `curl -H "X-aws-ec2-metadata-token: $TOKEN" http://169.254.169.254/latest/meta-data/security-groups` returns the ACTUAL attached SG name (launch-wizard-1); always verify attached SG via IMDSv2 before editing SG inbound rules; orphan SGs from prior wizard runs are common and visually indistinguishable. (d) **Lovable's framework default for new projects is NOT plain Vite** — defaults to `tanstack_start_ts_2026-05-12` SSR+Cloudflare Workers scaffold; requires explicit prompt "build target must be a static SPA where npm run build produces a single dist/ directory containing index.html at root plus assets/ folder" to convert; for AWS nginx-served deployments this conversion is mandatory pre-data-wiring. (e) **Env vars for client-side React apps in Vite are inlined at BUILD time not runtime** — `import.meta.env.VITE_*` becomes string literal in bundle; `.env.local` AWS-side at `/home/ssm-user/merdian-marketview/.env.local` is the canonical injection point because git pull won't overwrite gitignored files; verification via `grep -o '<project-ref>' /var/www/marketview/assets/*.js | wc -l ≥ 1` after redeploy. (f) **Lovable can't push commits — operator workstation needed for `git rm --cached .env` to remove committed `.env` from history** — this is a permanent limitation of Lovable's git environment; for hygiene-only fixes (anon key in public repo) operator must handle locally and push. (g) **Schema adaptations Lovable makes during data wiring are reasonable and need verification** — Lovable adapted spec to actual schema for `ict_zones` (no valid_to → order by detected_at_ts), `signal_snapshots` (no tier → use entry_quality), pin/accel views (pin_lower/upper not what spec assumed); each adaptation correct against live column-list audit. redeploy script needs `git fetch + git pull` not just `git pull`. **CARRY_FORWARD_TO_S40:** P0 operator local `git rm --cached .env` + push to remove anon key from public GitHub repo (TD-S39-NEW-3); P0b smoke_probe_marketview_surfaces.py first run (anon vs service-key divergence detector); Fix: `COALESCE(p.level, (p.zone_low + p.zone_high) / 2.0)` as formation anchor — uses zone midpoint for OB/FVG, scalar level for SWEEP. **Exp 53 v2 (post-fix) HEADLINE finding:** **M5 BEAR_FVG entries within 0.25% of flip level are anti-edge.** Train NIFTY p1 N=85 WR 35.3% mean PnL_EOD **-10.22** median -12.15; Train SENSEX p1 N=91 WR 35.2% mean **-9.71**; Holdout NIFTY p1 N=12 WR 33.3% mean **-38.24**; Holdout SENSEX p1 N=12 WR **16.7%** mean **-37.71**. Initial smoke-fire PASS cross-symbol: NIFTY run_id `082928a6-3b85-4427-a841-b6a569dcdf76` 144 strikes abs_diff=9.8e-11 Cr against total `gamma_metrics.net_gex`; SENSEX run_id `2566ae3a-cc70-43aa-9bfa-421d38eb3fb2` 261 strikes abs_diff=1.2e-14 Cr; sign convention validated; ADR-014 ACCEPTED. **Quant escalation post smoke-fire surfaced architectural defect:** derived booleans fire on 39% of NIFTY rows / 20% of SENSEX rows = near-zero information content as a marker; booleans were designed as "strike has structural significance" markers but threshold relativity makes them positive on too many rows to discriminate signal from noise; same finding generalizes — derived booleans at write layer almost always misclassify when their threshold is regime-conditional. Concurrent finding: single `gamma` column collapses IV skew evidence material at NIFTY 24050 ATM `gamma_call=0.00164` vs `gamma_put=0.00234` (+43% PE-richer = put-skew regime) — collapsing to a single column destroys regime classification capability. **ADR-015 ACCEPTED supersedes ADR-014 same session** — schema v2 redesign: drop `gamma` (replaced by `gamma_call` + `gamma_put` to preserve IV skew); drop `is_local_max` + `is_flip_zone` + `is_pin_candidate_bool` (derivations belong in read layer as SQL views not write layer columns); keep 12-column minimum-sufficient-statistic shape `(run_id, strike, expiry_date, symbol, ts, spot, gamma_call, gamma_put, oi_total_calls, oi_total_puts, gex_cr, source_table)`; UNIQUE (run_id, strike, expiry_date) preserved; sign convention preserved. **Schema migration:** `sql/2026-05-25_enh80_schema_v2_migration.sql` (TRUNCATE existing + ALTER TABLE drop 4 cols + add 2 cols + reload PostgREST schema cache); migration timing was safe because v1 had no consumers locked against the boolean columns yet — v1 patch trail + backup preserved for git audit, no v2-to-v1 rollback path required because there is nothing built on v1 to roll back. **`patch_s37_enh80_writer_v2.py` (marker `# ENH-80 (S37) v2`, backup `compute_gamma_metrics_local_PRE_S37_v2.py`, 18,053 bytes)** deployed against migrated schema with auto-refuse guard on v1 marker presence to prevent accidental re-application of v1. (d) **Per-tuple range-prefetch is canonical pattern for chain reads at scale** — group I/O by tuple, amortize query overhead. (e) **Empirical expiry calendar beats DOW rules** — NSE/BSE 2025-09-01 swap + ~15% holiday-shifted + same-week double expiries defeat any pure DOW formula. (f) **Median PnL universally negative on a cell with 80%+ spot WR is a source-table smell, not an edge property** — investigate before concluding "no edge." Third diagnostic step at 18:00+ IST after market close revealed independent root causes via log tail of restarted feeder showing `Supabase write error 500: {code:57014,message:canceling statement due to statement timeout}`. **Fix sequence:** (1) Step 1 consumer-restart `pkill -9 -f ws_feed_zerodha.py + nohup python3 ws_feed_zerodha.py >> logs/ws_feed.log 2>&1 &` (Root Cause A); (2) Step 2 reference-layer catch-up `python3 refresh_equity_intraday_last.py` (09:05 IST cron had fired with broken token and failed silently); (3) Step 3 `pkill -9 -f ws_feed_zerodha.py + TRUNCATE public.market_ticks` (62 GB → 856 kB in <1s; DDL primitive — DELETE itself would have timed out at this size; TRUNCATE rebuilds indexes inline, no REINDEX or VACUUM needed) + restart feeder; (4) Step 4 retention cron replacement `cron.unschedule(45) + cron.schedule('prune-market-ticks', '*/30 * * * 1-5', delete-where-ts-less-than-1-hour) → jobid 46` (cadence 1/day → 1/30min, horizon 2days → 1hour decouples worst-case DELETE workload from cron cadence; breadth ingest reads only last 10 min so 1-hour horizon is safe; worst-case DELETE workload now ~1 GB per 30-min run, well inside statement_timeout). **Cost incurred:** market_breadth_intraday 0 rows for 2026-05-14 not recoverable (10-min rolling window is ephemeral by design); signal_snapshots.breadth_regime NULL for all 697 signals 2026-05-14 not recoverable (ADR-008 replay reads market_breadth_intraday so also can't reconstruct); operator hours ~3h incident response; trading hours degraded from 09:15 IST but hybrid discretionary process compensated, no live trades on bad data per operator confirmation. **Concurrent Dhan 429 storm (TD-080 3rd documented occurrence):** 99/808 `ingest_option_chain_local.py` cycles failed with `status=429 path=/v2/optionchain response={data:{805:Too many requests. Codified as: build expected-time series in UTC at actual UTC times (e.g. `'2026-05-14 03:45:00+00'::timestamptz` for 09:15 IST trading-start) and let join handle TZ conversion in output formatting only; never use `timezone()` cast to construct IST series from wall-clock string literal. **Real 17 gaps after corrected query:** 10:21-10:24 (4 min), 10:27 (1 min), 10:42-10:44 (3 min), SENSEX 15:29 closing; `capture_spot_1m_v2.py` `RUNNING` (never-finalized) entry at 10:24:58 IST = smoking gun for first cluster; pattern repeats at 10:42-10:44; both clusters precede Dhan 429 storm by ~25 min suggesting same token+endpoint stress at lower amplitude before rate-limit threshold tripped. **Backfill execution:** MALPHA-side via `backfill_spot_zerodha.py` after file repair (sed had corrupted multi-line `BACKFILL_DATES = [...]` list literal during earlier attempt; surgical Python heredoc fix preserved valid syntax + AST-validated); 750 rows idempotent upsert to `hist_spot_bars_1m` (375 NIFTY + 375 SENSEX, net 17 new); mirror SQL `INSERT INTO market_spot_snapshots ... Topology §3 + §7.1 + §8.2 + §1 row updated. **CRITICAL LESSONS Session 28:** (a) **Cross-Python-version stdlib semantics (B22)** — Local Python 3.12 ≠ AWS Python 3.10 for `datetime.fromisoformat()` microsecond precision. Python 3.10 accepts only 3 or 6-digit microseconds; Python 3.12 permissive. Supabase serializes PG timestamps with variable precision (2-7 digits). Local smoke test necessary but not sufficient — must verify on AWS. Canonical normalize-to-6-digits pattern via regex pad/truncate before `fromisoformat()`. Long-term: align Python versions across Local + AWS. Codified as CLAUDE.md B22 + Topology §6.9 new gotcha + Assumption Register §D.11.3. (b) **Phase 0 closure exercises surface residual defects (B23)** — Phase 0 closure (data backfills, schema reconciliations, replay validations) are defect-discovery surfaces. Budget for residual surfaces: scheduling a Phase 0 closure as "30-45 min backfill" routinely produces 3-5 hours of resolution work. Discovery rate is high because Phase 0 closure exercises stress-test code paths that production daily cadence doesn't exercise (backfill cohort sizes, off-hours timing, cross-version stdlib, schema drift). Build the closure exercise schedule with discovery budget, not just execution budget. Codified as CLAUDE.md B23 + Assumption Register §D.11.4. (c) **AWS shadow architecture being silently violated for 13 days is the consequence of "schema present, behavior absent" deployment** — `gamma_metrics_shadow` table existed since shadow runner deployed but no code wired the redirect; AWS shadow defaulted to writing production. For architectural separations that depend on flag/parameter wiring, verify the wiring is exercised end-to-end at deployment time. Schema-only proxies for separation are insufficient. Smoke test must include `actual_writes` telemetry. Topology §6.5 update + §6.8 new gotcha codify. (d) **PGRST204 schema cache errors after `ALTER TABLE` require explicit `NOTIFY pgrst, 'reload schema'`** — PostgREST caches schema for performance; does not auto-reload on DDL. Operational rule for any Supabase-served table receiving DDL. (e) **42P10 ON CONFLICT errors after `CREATE TABLE LIKE` indicate missing UNIQUE constraint, not missing column** — `CREATE TABLE ... LIKE` copies columns but not constraints unless `INCLUDING ALL`. When discovering post-deployment: `ALTER TABLE <shadow> ADD CONSTRAINT <name>_<cols>_key UNIQUE (<cols>)` is the surgical fix. (f) **Run_id-keyed retry pattern is canonical backfill recovery** — Each backfill row logged with `run_id` + status code; retry queue = `SELECT WHERE status='FAILED'`. Not re-run-the-entire-batch. ~5 min recovery on 60/587 failures via retry vs ~30-45 min full re-run. (g) **TD-NEW-10 closed-filed-in-error is canonical "audited live, confirmed intentional" closure pattern** — discovered un-audited process; filed as un-audited at S2; investigated; confirmed intentional; closed as filed-in-error with documentation gap filed separately as TD-NEW-11. Separates "real defect" from "documentation drift" cleanly. (h) **Operational drift after P0 closure is structural session shape; budget for it explicitly** — P0 closure in <20 min of session time; remainder of session is operational firefighting / discovery / emergent TD resolution. Not session-discipline failure; structural shape of post-deployment verification sessions. Plan next 4-6 hours as drift budget at session-start. **Files modified Session 28:** 2 production code patches (`compute_gamma_metrics_local.py` TD-NEW-12 + TD-NEW-4 + TD-NEW-13 = three edits one file, `run_merdian_shadow_runner.py` AWS wrapper TD-NEW-12 line 479) + 4 backup files preserved (`compute_gamma_metrics_local_PRE_TD-NEW-12.py`, `_PRE_TD-NEW-4.py`, `_PRE_TD-NEW-13.py`, `run_merdian_shadow_runner.py.bak_pre_TD-NEW-12`) + 4 patch scripts NEW (`fix_td_new_12_shadow_flag.py`, `fix_td_new_4_dte_uses_ts.py`, `fix_td_new_13_microsecond_normalize.py`, `fix_run_merdian_shadow_runner.py`) + 0 ADR drafts (ADR-005 + ADR-009 still pending per S25-S26 carry-forward) + 7 documentation files in S28 doc-close pack + 1 Enhancement Register file (ENH-84 + ENH-85 PROPOSED entries). **Schema changes:** `gamma_metrics_shadow` ALTER TABLE 7 columns ADD + UNIQUE constraint ADD + NOTIFY pgrst. **Cron / Tasks added:** None. (b) **Latent algorithm fragility surfaces only under input-shape change** — TD-NEW-2 was a stable computation against stable input for months; Dhan's response changed shape 2026-05-08 (spurious deep-ITM gamma values appearing where previously zero), exposing fragility that would never have surfaced under prior data conditions. Tests against prior data passed; new-data class-of-bugs the original implementation never anticipated. Defense-in-depth (Part A input filter + Part B algorithm hardening) shipped to prevent this class. (c) **Unit-scale bugs are silent when all consumers are sign-only** — TD-NEW-3 had been writing 10³-too-large values since the gamma engine deployed; never surfaced because no gate threshold consumed magnitude. Surfaced only via cross-comparison to source-material Cr values during sign audit. Codified as B21: when introducing magnitude-consuming gates, audit existing column unit conventions FIRST against source-of-truth references, before threshold tuning. (d) **Smoke test caught honest framing of fix architecture** — original framing called Part A + Part B "belt + suspenders." Smoke test demonstrated Part B alone insufficient against the specific bug pattern (cumulative plateau through bad-row region); honest reframing: Part A necessary, Part B hardening for class-of-future-bugs. Honest framing in code comments + commit message + carry-forward to ensure future operator doesn't assume defensive equivalence between parts. (e) **Source-material disagreement is not always inversion** — Ref 2 source-dashboard showed -976 Cr → -14,323 Cr FALLING; MERDIAN showed +56T-81T at same timestamps. Initially flagged as potential sign inversion. Resolution: source dashboard was showing PROJECTED dealer-flow scenario for hypothetical -1% spot move ("if spot drops 1%, dealers will sell ₹14,180 Cr"), not LIVE net GEX state. Two different metrics, both shown on the same dashboard panel — disagreement was reader-side categorisation error, not data error. Commit `5b94c78`, +8 lines, AST OK on Local + AWS. **TD-099 closed as filed-in-error** — Operator picked TD-099 (5 production audit scripts URL-encoding bug) at session opening; verification via URL-spy (intercepted `requests.get` calls) showed all 4 scripts in scope (`build_signal_market_path_audit_v1.py`, `build_signal_outcome_audit_local.py`, `build_signal_regret_log_v1.py`, `build_option_execution_outcomes_v1.py`) emit clean single-`?` URLs with proper encoding (`%2A`=`*`, `%2C`=`,`); 5th script `premium_outcome_writer.py` uses supabase Python client not raw requests — different code path entirely. TD-099 grep `requests.get.*SUPABASE.*params` matched both broken TD-097 form (URL with `?` AND params dict) and standard-correct form (clean URL + params dict only). **Filing rule:** "same anti-pattern in N other scripts" claims require URL-spy or runtime trace verification before priority assignment, not just grep matches. ~3 hours of unnecessary patching avoided. **CRITICAL LESSONS Session 26:** (a) **OI-18 class fix at one site does NOT close the class** — TD-097 dashboard fix S25 + TD-099 grep audit closed nothing real, TD-101 was the actual writer-side propagation the grep couldn't reach (anti-pattern buried in `supabase_select()` helper not URL construction). When fixing OI-18-class bugs the closure of the class requires runtime verification of every candidate site including writer-side helpers downstream of the symptom site, not just grep at request-side construction. Codified as B19. (b) **Production data on the live cohort over 24 documented days trumps research-cohort hypothesis** when they disagree directionally — Exp 20's evidence (5m-batch hist_pattern_signals cohort) does not survive translation to live signal cohort under current selection logic; default to disabling the parameter behind reversible flag, file as Assumption Register row, re-validate only with proper outcome metric on the cohort the parameter actually gates. First substantive application of §D.8.3 prospective parity check post-codification S25; flag drift criterion fired within 24 days well inside the 60-day prospective threshold. (c) **Reversible disablement (env flag, default OFF) > code removal** for hypothesis-falsified parameters — re-validation cost should be one experiment not one re-implementation; code paths that fail empirically are still valuable as documentation of what was tried. (d) **Gates guarded on `not None` checks of writer-produced values need parallel writer-cadence diagnostics** at gate-promotion time — ENH-55's silent failure produced telemetrically identical output to "gate not firing because ret_session in neutral band"; only writer-cadence assertion (`SELECT COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE col IS NULL) FROM table WHERE date = today` should approach 0) would have surfaced the regression at cycle-1 not at retrospective audit. (e) **Same-session TD close discipline** — TD-101 NEW S1 → RESOLVED commit `3cb84e2` within Session 26 (TD-097 was S25 precedent; TD-101 second instance); the audit trail (NEW + RESOLVED in same session) matters for future sessions reading the register, both blocks recorded in tech_debt.md. 2026-04-28 · `pending` · Session 12 (documentation/philosophy -- gamma dashboard analysis + ADR-002 + register overhaul): Gamma dashboard built by a successful options writer (short-gamma seller) analysed against MERDIAN Gamma Engine. Six structural gaps identified: (1) MERDIAN stores scalar GEX metrics only -- no per-strike histogram, so pin zones, acceleration zones, and local vs aggregate divergence are all invisible; (2) binary LONG/SHORT regime based on net_gex sign misclassifies PINNED sessions where local GEX around spot is strongly positive but net GEX is negative -- documented in Appendix D, Exp 23 is the validation path; (3) no acceleration zone as a first-class engine output (flip level stored but not the zone above it where short-gamma writers are trapped); (4) direction only, no force -- dealer Cr flow magnitude is the actual edge, not regime label; (5) no regime velocity -- max gamma migration and gex_velocity are untracked; (6) DTE used as binary execution gate only, not as force multiplier. ADR-002 authored (docs/decisions/ADR-002-market-structure-philosophy.md): six principles P1 (zones not points), P2 (force not direction), P3 (know where sellers panic), P4 (regime velocity), P5 (local beats aggregate), P6 (DTE is force multiplier). Capital scaling roadmap settled: Phase 1 = naked options buying (~25,000 lot capacity ceiling before market impact), Phase 2 = debit spreads at ceiling, Phase 3 = defined-risk selling (NOT naked) requiring full P1-P5 implementation first. GEX weekly time-series storage decision: store per-strike GEX at 5-min cadence across full expiry week -- data already in option_chain_snapshots, aggregation only, ~15,600 rows/day. ENH-80 (per-strike GEX time-series + zone bounds -- PROPOSED), ENH-81 (dealer flow simulator + regime velocity -- PROPOSED), ENH-82 (PINNED gamma regime -- PROPOSED, blocked on Exp 23), ENH-83 (DTE-adjusted force multiplier -- PROPOSED, deferred Phase 1.5+) filed. 2026-04-28 · `pending` · Session 11 (single concern — ICT research agenda): Full experimental session. 11 experiments run (Exp 34–41B). Concern: identify new intraday and multi-day edges by testing ICT liquidity concepts (BSL/SSL, PO3/AMD, weekly HTF context) against 12 months of NIFTY/SENSEX bar data. 7 edges proven, 4 concepts ruled out. Key findings: (1) Naked PDH/PDL sweeps = FAIL (Exp 34, WR=11%). (2) PDH first-sweep filtered = 93.3% bearish EOD WR (Exp 35C PASS, N=15). (3) PDL first-sweep filtered = 72% bullish EOD (Exp 35C PASS, N=25). (4) PDH DTE<3 → current-week PE: T+1D WR=72.7%; current-week beats next-week (mean +125% SENSEX, Exp 35D PASS). Ruled out: PO3 as OB amplifier (Exp 36 FAIL), London kill zone combined (Exp 37 partial — 13:30-14:00 BEAR_OB 77.8% promising), weekly sweep unrefined (Exp 39 FAIL). Core structural insight: PO3 sweep = session bias setter only; trade is BEAR_OB MIDDAY (bearish sessions) or BULL_OB AFTERNOON SENSEX (bullish sessions). MAE analysis (Exp 41): MAE P90=94pts NIFTY / 373pts SENSEX — SENSEX short-DTE options not viable at sweep entry. Entry timing: T+0 always beats waiting. ret_30m stored as percentage points (÷100 for decimal). Kelly fractions capped at 5-8% until N=30 live events. ## 2026-04-22 — engineering / operations — Session 5: OI series permanent closure (6 OIs closed) + PS 5.1 encoding fix

**Goal:** Close all 6 open OI items (18, 19, 20, 21, 22, 23) carried forward from Session 3+4 resume prompt, so the OI-* namespace can be permanently retired per Documentation Protocol v2 Rule 5 (`no_new_oi_register`). Each closure to be surgical, single-purpose, with ast.parse() validated patch scripts per V18H governance.

**Session type:** engineering / operations

**Completed:**

OI-22 CLOSED — Dhan transient-failure vs auth-failure alert routing (commit d130044, preceded by 2b6e2bb short commit):
- Root cause: `AUTH_FAILURE_PATTERNS` in `run_option_snapshot_intraday_runner.py` included the substring `"accessToken"`, which matched any ingest stdout/stderr that printed request headers during transient network timeouts. Result: transient timeouts produced `OPTION_AUTH_BREAK` Telegram alerts, falsely suggesting a token refresh was required.
- Fix: removed `"accessToken"` from `AUTH_FAILURE_PATTERNS`. Added new `TRANSIENT_FAILURE_PATTERNS` list (ReadTimeout, ConnectTimeout, ConnectionError, Max retries exceeded, HTTPSConnectionPool, Read timed out, Connection aborted) and `_is_transient_failure()` helper. Dispatcher now checks transient first; issues distinct `OPTION_TRANSIENT_FAIL` alert that explicitly tells the operator NOT to refresh the token. Auth path retightened to "Dhan 401 / token invalid" wording.
- Patch script: `fix_oi22_transient_vs_auth.py` with ast.parse() guard.

OI-23 CLOSED — MERDIAN_SIGNAL_V4 docstring/code default drift (commit 873a866):
- Code default is `"1"` (V4 on) since commit e986cbb post-ENH-53/55 validation. Docstring block in `build_trade_signal_local.py` lines 59-64 still said "Default is off. Enable explicitly for shadow sessions. Flip default only after 5 clean shadow sessions per Change Protocol."
- Fix: rewrote the Flag comment block to document current state (default "1", V3 escape hatch via `MERDIAN_SIGNAL_V4=0`). No code change.
- Patch script: `fix_oi23_signal_v4_docstring.py`.

OI-20 CLOSED — PS 5.1 UTF-8 BOM injection into git commit subjects (commit 93d2d80, disposition note at `docs/session_notes/20260422_oi20_encoding_disposition.md`):
- Finding: commits 3a22735 through d15c494 (9 Session 3+4 commits) carry literal UTF-8 BOM (`EF BB BF`) bytes embedded in commit subjects, confirmed via `git log --format="%s" | Format-Hex`. Not a display artifact.
- Root cause: PowerShell 5.1 default console encoding is cp850 / cp1252 (WindowsCodePage=1252). When `git commit -m "..."` received a message containing non-ASCII (em-dash —), PS 5.1's pipeline transcoding emitted UTF-8-WITH-BOM and git stored the bytes verbatim. `i18n.commitEncoding` was unset.
- Disposition: history NOT rewritten. Force-push cost across Local + MERDIAN AWS + MeridianAlpha consumer exceeds benefit for cosmetic BOMs. Commit hashes preserved as audit trail.
- Fix forward: PowerShell `$PROFILE` created at `C:\Users\balan\Documents\WindowsPowerShell\Microsoft.PowerShell_profile.ps1` forcing `$OutputEncoding`, `Console.OutputEncoding`, `Console.InputEncoding` to `UTF8Encoding::new($false)` — UTF-8 without BOM. Git global config: `i18n.commitEncoding=utf-8`, `i18n.logOutputEncoding=utf-8`. Verification commit confirmed no BOM (subject starts at byte `4F`, not `EF BB BF`).
- Residual limitation documented: PS 5.1 still cannot pass non-ASCII characters through `-m "..."` argv serialization (em-dash degraded to `?`). Going-forward discipline: ASCII only in commit subjects, or use `git commit -F message.txt` for non-ASCII.

OI-19 CLOSED — Out of scope (commit 7a4bae5, disposition note at `docs/session_notes/20260422_oi19_out_of_scope.md`):
- Resume prompt carried OI-19 as "MeridianAlpha kernel reboot (non-urgent)".
- Disposition: MeridianAlpha is a separate system from MERDIAN (separate repo, scope limited to corporate actions data and Zerodha token refresh per V19 §3.1). Its host-level maintenance is not tracked in the MERDIAN register. No action required; item should not have been filed under MERDIAN OI.

OI-18 CLOSED — Dashboard preopen false-negative (commit 6917094):
- Investigation disproved the resume-prompt framing ("capture_spot_1m doesn't set is_pre_market=true on pre-open bars"). Live SQL confirmed pre-open bars at 09:05 and 09:14 IST are written correctly to `hist_spot_bars_1m` with `is_pre_market=false`. Every consumer across the codebase (ICT detection, MTF bars, HTF zones, experiments) queries `.eq("is_pre_market", False)`. The `is_pre_market` column is effectively vestigial — always False writer-side, always filtered on False consumer-side.
- Actual root cause (two bugs in `merdian_live_dashboard.get_preopen_status()`): (a) `sb_get("market_spot_snapshots", "select=ts,spot,symbol&order=ts.asc&limit=10")` returned the 10 oldest rows in an ever-growing table, not today's rows — permanent NOT CAPTURED after day one; (b) window filter `dt.hour == 9 and dt.minute < 9` covered 09:00-09:08 only, missed the 09:14 bar.
- Fix: query today's rows via `ts>=start-of-IST-day UTC ISO` lower bound, widen window to `dt.minute < 15` (pre-open closes at market open 09:15), return up to 6 rows instead of 3.
- Not fixed (deliberate): the vestigial `is_pre_market` column. Deferred as a separate cleanup opportunity outside this OI closure.
- Patch script: `fix_oi18_dashboard_preopen.py`.

OI-21 CLOSED — refresh_dhan_token hardening (commit f7b9366):
- Investigation disproved the resume-prompt framing ("silent fail when invoked by Task Scheduler"). Post-OI-16 scheduled task runs succeed: LastTaskResult=0 at 2026-04-21 18:15:06, `runtime/token_status.json` shows `success: true, refreshed_at_iso: 2026-04-21T18:15:07.661476+05:30`. Historical `'python' is not recognized` entries in `logs/dhan_token_refresh.log` are pre-OI-16 ghosts already resolved by absolute Python path fix.
- Residual real bug in `refresh_dhan_token.py` main() retry path: line showed `print("...Waiting 30s...")` but `_time.sleep(120)`. The 120-second sleep matched Dhan's 2-minute token-generation rate-limit window exactly; the retry landed on the boundary and frequently tripped the `"Token can be generated once every 2 minutes"` error. This internal cascade accounted for the rate-limit entries observed in the log.
- Three fixes applied: (1) retry sleep 120s → 30s (one TOTP window, well under rate-limit boundary); (2) idempotency guard at main() entry — reads `token_status.json`, if last success < 90s old prints `[IDEMPOTENT]` and returns 0 without calling Dhan, protects against any double-caller (scheduled task + dashboard button at line 57 of `merdian_live_dashboard.py` + TOTP retry self-fire + preflight stages); (3) explicit rate-limit handling in both first-attempt and retry paths — writes `token_status.json` with error, returns distinct exit code 2 (recently-refreshed-elsewhere, not a failure).
- Patch script: `fix_oi21_token_refresh_hardening.py`.

**Governance outcome:**

- All 6 OIs (OI-18 through OI-23) from Session 3+4 resume prompt are now CLOSED. The OI-* namespace is permanently retired per Documentation Protocol v2 Rule 5 (`no_new_oi_register`, governance rules line 1664 of `merdian_reference.json`). Future operational issues route to Enhancement Register (ENH-N, persistent) or `merdian_reference.json` `open_items` C-N (critical production) only.
- Confirmed during this session: Session 3+4 OI-16/17/24/25/26/27 entries in session_log were never formally added to `merdian_reference.json` `open_items` — consistent with Rule 5. They functioned as session-local labels for tracked work, not persistent register entries. Same disposition applies to OI-18/19/20/21/22/23: session-local labels, closed within the same session, no register entry required.

**Open after session:**
- Documentation debt closeout (this session's primary next step):
  - V19A appendix — consolidated coverage of Session 1+2 (2026-04-20: ENH-66/68/71 outage + architecture) + Session 3+4 (2026-04-21: ENH-72 + OI-24/26/27 fixes + backfill + ICT rebuild + Task Scheduler repair) + Session 5 (2026-04-22: 6 OI closures + PS 5.1 encoding fix).   - Enhancement Register overhaul (on-disk v7 stops at ENH-59, missing ENH-60 through ENH-74+). New version to reconcile.

- Session 7 (ENH-67/69/73): dashboard + alerts — downstream

**Files changed (core/):**

**Environment changes:**

- Git global config: `i18n.commitEncoding=utf-8`, `i18n.logOutputEncoding=utf-8`.

**Schema changes:** none

Fix (a): replaced with data-driven should_rebuild_1h_zones(sb, symbol) — checks ict_htf_zones directly, rebuilds once per hour per symbol regardless of cycle schedule. Fix (b): moved __main__ block to end of file. Smoke confirmed 4 1H zones now visible in ict_htf_zones (first time ever). Commit d15c494.

Pipeline propagates the Dhan-returned raw IV correctly through every stage. ## 2026-04-20 — live_canary / code_debug / architecture — Outage + re-engineering programme Sessions 1+2

**Goal:** Diagnose and fix the morning's 3-hour silent pipeline outage; ship the architectural foundation (ENH-66 holiday-gate root cause + ENH-68 tactical runner env reload + ENH-71 write-contract layer) to prevent a recurrence of the bug class.

**Session type:** live_canary / code_debug / architecture

**Completed:**
  - **Morning outage diagnosed end-to-end.** 09:15 IST: seven production scripts silently exited "Market holiday" on a trading day. Root cause: V18G holiday-gate logic treats `open_time IS NULL` as "market closed"; `trading_calendar` row auto-inserted by `merdian_start.py` carried `{trade_date, is_open=True}` only — `open_time` and `close_time` NULL. Scripts exited cleanly with code 0. Dashboard, Task Scheduler, supervisor all green. Pipeline flowing zero rows for 3 hours until 11:39 IST when the row was patched live via direct Supabase PATCH.
  - **Second compounding bug surfaced at 11:26 IST.** Dhan token expired ~10:06 IST (OPTION_AUTH_BREAK Telegram alert fired). `refresh_dhan_token.py` updated `.env` at 11:00:10 IST successfully, but the runner process (PID 18036, started 09:15:34) held the stale in-memory token from its startup `load_dotenv()` call. Every cycle 401 from 11:26 to 12:26 IST. Only `merdian_stop.py` + `merdian_start.py` fixed it. 60 additional minutes lost.
  - **Pipeline recovered 12:26+ IST.** NIFTY NO_FLIP DO_NOTHING conf=16, SENSEX NO_FLIP DO_NOTHING conf=28. No bad trades taken during the outage window.
  - **Post-mortem conducted honestly.** Central insight: every symptom traces to ONE absence — MERDIAN has no write-contract enforcement. Scripts declare success by exit code 0; nothing verifies they did their actual job. Preflight probe-tests pass while pipeline is already broken. Dashboard green lights based on "last row wrote recently," not "expected rows wrote this cycle."
  - **6-session re-engineering programme approved.** Sessions 1 through 6 sequenced: stop the bleeding, write-contract layer, propagate, preflight rewrite, live config, dashboard truth + alerts. Each session produces own commit chain, register entry, replay-validation. No merges without validation paste in chat transcript.
  - **Session 1 shipped (ENH-66, ENH-68 tactical).** Two patches, two commits:
    - Commit `8f83859` — ENH-66: `ensure_calendar_row()` in `merdian_start.py` patched at INSERT path (include open_time/close_time for weekday rows) and existing-row PATCH path (backfill NULL times). UTF-8 BOM stripped as side effect. Validation: DELETE calendar row → re-creates with times populated; `capture_spot_1m.py` writes rows instead of silent-exit; regression test `is_open=False` → correct holiday exit.
    - Commit `b195499` — ENH-68 tactical: guarded `load_dotenv(override=True)` at top of `run_full_cycle()` in `run_option_snapshot_intraday_runner.py`. One reload per 5-minute cycle. Log line per cycle for audit trail. Graceful degradation if python-dotenv unavailable. Strategic replacement filed as ENH-74 for Session 5.
  - **Session 2 shipped (ENH-71 write-contract layer foundation).** Commit `260c7d0`. Three deliverables:
    - SQL: `public.script_execution_log` table with closed-set CHECK constraint on `exit_reason` (11 values). Partial indexes on `contract_met=false` and non-SUCCESS rows. View `public.v_script_execution_health_30m` for dashboard/alert consumption. RLS policies.
    - Code: `core.execution_log.ExecutionLog` helper class. API: `record_write(table, n)`, `exit_with_reason(reason, ...)`, `complete(notes)`. Opening row INSERT at construction. Finalise PATCH with computed `contract_met`. `atexit` hook catches crashes → `exit_reason='CRASH'` with traceback. Invalid reasons coerced to CRASH. Best-effort writes; never raises into caller.
    - Reference implementation: `capture_spot_1m.py` converted. Declares `expected_writes={market_spot_snapshots: 2, hist_spot_bars_1m: 2}`. Six exit paths classified.
  - **ENH-71 validated live against Supabase (6 tests).** Empty table + accessible view + CHECK constraint rejected INVALID_REASON; smoke SUCCESS met=True; contract violation (1 of 3) met=False; atexit crash path CRASH; HOLIDAY_GATE early exit met=False; live run of converted `capture_spot_1m.py` SUCCESS met=True 2+2 writes 1114ms. **Replay of today's exact outage**: flipped `is_open=False`, row recorded `reason=HOLIDAY_GATE met=False expected={...: 2, ...: 2} actual={} notes='trading_calendar says closed'`. Today's silent exit is now a dashboard-visible, alertable row.
  - **Enhancement Register updated (commit `7174690`).** Previous commit `ccaa418` had compressed many ENH-01..65 entry blocks when adding ENH-66..74. Recovered via `git checkout HEAD~1 -- ...` to restore full 88107-byte / 1737-line original. Applied `append_enh66_to_74.py` — strictly-additive patch with 7 anchor-validated edits, uniqueness-checked, size-must-grow guard. Net: 1737 → 2049 lines (+312), all ENH-01..65 prose untouched. Added 9 new entry blocks (ENH-66..74), MERDIAN Re-engineering Programme section, 2026-04-20 change log row, trailer update.

**Open after session:**

## 2026-04-13 (late evening) — engineering — Phase 4A + ENH-02/04/06/07 + Signal Engine

**Goal:** Wire options flow into signal engine, build Phase 4A execution layer, close remaining Tier 1 ENH items.

**Session type:** engineering

**Completed:**

ENH-02/04/07 — Options flow wired into confidence scoring:
- `build_trade_signal_local.py`: fetches `options_flow_snapshots` each cycle
- PCR BEARISH+BUY_PE → +5, PCR BULLISH+BUY_CE → +5, contra → -4
- SKEW FEAR+BUY_PE → +4, SKEW GREED+BUY_CE → +4
- FLOW PE_ACTIVE+BUY_PE → +3, FLOW CE_ACTIVE+BUY_CE → +3
- ENH-07: basis_pct note added (futures premium/discount vs spot)
- Max lift on aligned signal: +12 confidence
- All stored in raw JSONB (no DDL needed)

ENH-06 — Pre-trade cost filter:
- `build_trade_signal_local.py`: validates lot sizing against capital at signal time
- Reads capital_tracker, estimates lot cost via estimate_lot_cost()
- If deployed > allocated × 1.10: reduces to 1 lot, adds caution
- Stores enh06_capital_ok, enh06_allocated, enh06_lot_cost in raw JSONB

Phase 4A — Manual execution layer:
- `merdian_trade_logger.py`: CLI trade logger. Reads latest signal, prompts entry price, writes trade_log + exit_alerts rows. Also handles --show (open trades) and --close (exit + PnL)
- `merdian_exit_monitor.py`: polls exit_alerts every 30s, fires console + Telegram alert at T+30m
- `merdian_signal_dashboard.py`: LOG TRADE button (green, appears when action ≠ DO_NOTHING), CLOSE TRADE button (always visible), modal dialogs, POST /log_trade + /close_trade endpoints
- `merdian_pm.py`: exit_monitor added to PROCESSES dict
- `merdian_start.py`: exit_monitor added to startup sequence

## 2026-04-06 — live_canary / code_debug / architecture — First Live Session + Architecture Repairs

**Goal:** Run first live market session (NIFTY/SENSEX options pipeline) and repair all root-cause failures discovered during the session.

**Session type:** live_canary / code_debug / architecture

**Completed:**

Live session:
- Runner started manually at 09:26 IST after calendar and syntax fixes (first cycle 09:30)
- NIFTY: BUY_PE action=48 confidence, trade_allowed=False (VIX panic gate >25 correctly blocked)
- SENSEX: DO_NOTHING, confidence=36
- VIX: 26.41 — PANIC regime, 100th percentile, VIX_UPTREND all session
- SMDM: NIFTY squeeze_score=4, SQUEEZE pattern active
- Full pipeline completed: options → gamma → volatility → momentum → market_state → signal → options_flow → momentum_v2 → SMDM → structural_alerts → shadow_v3
- AWS shadow runner manually started 09:46 IST, ran until 15:30 IST market close

Post-market architecture repairs:
- trading_calendar.py full rewrite — rule-based. Old design required manual row per date; missing row = system failure (root cause of today's morning failure). New: weekdays open by default, weekends closed by computation, NSE holidays are the only stored exceptions. No manual date insertion ever required again.
- trading_calendar.json rebuilt — holidays-only format. 23 NSE holiday entries for 2025-2026. Old 371-line manually maintained sessions list replaced.
- merdian_live_dashboard.py full rewrite (v2) — session state computed live from calendar (never stale), token block with expiry countdown, pre-open block (09:00-09:08) with spot capture status, pipeline stages showing actual values (spot, VIX, regime, signal action), breadth block with advances/declines, AWS shadow runner block via Supabase, action buttons with inline result within 5s (no click and pray), cp1252 encoding fixed for Windows.
- refresh_dhan_token.py — added runtime/token_status.json write after every attempt. Added TOTP retry: waits 30s and retries with next TOTP window on Invalid TOTP error.
- run_merdian_shadow_runner.py — breadth ingest disabled on AWS. Both Local and AWS were hitting the same Dhan token simultaneously causing 56/56 chunks returning 429 all day. AWS shadow is read-only for breadth. Also added write_cycle_status_to_supabase() — writes cycle_ok, breadth_coverage, per_symbol status to system_config table after each cycle for dashboard consumption.
- run_option_snapshot_intraday_runner.py — CREATE_NO_WINDOW flag added to subprocess calls. Eliminates 25-30 terminal windows flashing per 5-minute cycle.
- Task Scheduler MERDIAN_Live_Dashboard — updated with PYTHONIOENCODING=utf-8.

**Open after session:**
- C-07b confirmed: pre-open capture gap — supervisor task fires at 09:14, misses 09:00-09:08 window. Architectural fix needed.
- Shadow gate count: verify 5/10 after today
- Supabase disk usage: unverified post-session (was 9.5GB pre-session)
- ENH-35: run_validation_analysis.py — next build priority
- ENH-36: hist_* to live promotion pipeline — after ENH-35

**Files changed:** trading_calendar.py (full rewrite), trading_calendar.json (full rewrite), merdian_live_dashboard.py (full rewrite v2), refresh_dhan_token.py (token_status.json + TOTP retry), run_option_snapshot_intraday_runner.py (CREATE_NO_WINDOW), run_merdian_shadow_runner.py (breadth disabled + Supabase status write)
